# EvaLuate Lua API reference

_Generated by `--emit-api` for **Evaluate 0.8.0+8d784df185af8b81ebcece8c7029d8893699eb55** on **Godot 4.6-stable (official)**. Do not edit by hand â€” regenerate with `godot --headless --path . -- --emit-api downloads/spec`._

Every `.evt`/`.node.evt` script runs in a capability sandbox. Always available: `std`, `godot`, the safe language primitives, and (in node scripts) `self` plus `params`. Everything else must be declared in frontmatter `apis:`. For IDE autocomplete, point lua-language-server at the `luacats/` files.

## Always-available primitives

`assert`, `error`, `getmetatable`, `ipairs`, `math`, `next`, `pairs`, `print`, `rawequal`, `rawget`, `rawlen`, `rawset`, `select`, `setmetatable`, `string`, `table`, `tonumber`, `tostring`, `type`

**Deliberately withheld** (absent from every sandbox): `os`, `io`, `pcall`.

## std.* (always available)

### `std.color(r, g, b, a)`

Fields: `r: number`, `g: number`, `b: number`, `a: number`


### `std.linked_list()`

- `:push_front(v: any)`
- `:push_back(v: any)`
- `:pop_front()`
- `:pop_back()`
- `:front()` â†’ `any`
- `:back()` â†’ `any`
- `:size()` â†’ `integer`

### `std.vec2(x, y)`

Fields: `x: number`, `y: number`

- `:length()` â†’ `number`
- `:copy()` â†’ `std.vec2`

### `std.vec3(x, y, z)`

Fields: `x: number`, `y: number`, `z: number`

- `:length()` â†’ `number`
- `:copy()` â†’ `std.vec3`

### `std.vector()`

- `:push_back(v: any)`
- `:pop_back()`
- `:get(i: integer)` â†’ `any`
- `:set(i: integer, v: any)`
- `:size()` â†’ `integer`
- `:clear()`

## Capability apis (declare in `apis:`)

### `input`

- `input.is_down(...)`

### `save`

- `save.delete(...)`
- `save.get(...)`
- `save.set(...)`

### `scene`

- `scene.add(...)`
- `scene.change(...)`
- `scene.current(...)`
- `scene.find(...)`

### `sql`

- `sql.exec(...)`
- `sql.exec_async(...)`
- `sql.flush(...)`
- `sql.query(...)`
- `sql.query_row(...)`
- `sql.snapshot(...)`
- `sql.transaction(...)`

### `world`

The persistent global-root Node (a wrapped godot instance, not a table). Use any Node method/property â€” e.g. world:add_child(node). Survives scene switches.

## Lifecycle hooks (`register:`)

- **system** (`.evt`): `on_start`, `on_load`, `on_unload`, `on_quit`, `on_enter`, `on_exit`, `on_focus_in`, `on_focus_out`, `on_pause`, `on_resume`, `on_update`, `on_physics_update`, `on_input`
- **node** (`.node.evt`, `self`-bound): `on_attach`, `on_load`, `on_unload`, `on_update`, `on_physics_update`, `on_input`, `on_exit`, `on_quit`, `on_focus_in`, `on_focus_out`, `on_pause`, `on_resume`

## Frontmatter keys

`config`, `apis`, `register`, `returns`, `params`, `assets`, `scenes`

`returns:` grammar â€” `<name>  |  <name>: 'get set <type>'  (read-only omits 'set')`

`params:` grammar â€” `<name>: <type> | <name>: <default> | <name>: '<type> = <default>'  (node scripts only; types: number/string/bool/list/table/any; no default = required; the scene supplies values via `params = {..}` on the node)`

## Variant structs (named-field / positional tables)

Read as tables; assigned back type-aware. All-scalar structs use a positional array; composite structs use a `_type`-tagged table.

- **Vector2** â€” positional `[x, y]`: `x, y`
- **Vector2I** â€” positional `[x, y]`: `x, y`
- **Rect2** â€” composite `{ _type = "Rect2", â€¦ }`: `position, size, end`
- **Rect2I** â€” composite `{ _type = "Rect2I", â€¦ }`: `position, size, end`
- **Vector3** â€” positional `[x, y, z]`: `x, y, z`
- **Vector3I** â€” positional `[x, y, z]`: `x, y, z`
- **Transform2D** â€” composite `{ _type = "Transform2D", â€¦ }`: `x, y, origin`
- **Vector4** â€” positional `[x, y, z, w]`: `x, y, z, w`
- **Vector4I** â€” positional `[x, y, z, w]`: `x, y, z, w`
- **Plane** â€” composite `{ _type = "Plane", â€¦ }`: `normal, d, x, y, z`
- **Quaternion** â€” positional `[x, y, z, w]`: `x, y, z, w`
- **Aabb** â€” composite `{ _type = "Aabb", â€¦ }`: `position, size, end`
- **Basis** â€” composite `{ _type = "Basis", â€¦ }`: `row0, row1, row2`
- **Transform3D** â€” composite `{ _type = "Transform3D", â€¦ }`: `basis, origin`
- **Projection** â€” composite `{ _type = "Projection", â€¦ }`: `x, y, z, w`
- **Color** â€” positional `[r, g, b, a]`: `r, g, b, a`
